# What are the rules for credits consumption? And how can I obtain them? | Manus Help Center

[Skip to main content](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711097-what-are-the-rules-for-credits-consumption-and-how-can-i-obtain-them#main-content)

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711097-what-are-the-rules-for-credits-consumption-and-how-can-i-obtain-them#h_a43da6039d)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711097-what-are-the-rules-for-credits-consumption-and-how-can-i-obtain-them#h_7b459051ff)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711097-what-are-the-rules-for-credits-consumption-and-how-can-i-obtain-them#h_3dbe093a6a)

[All Collections](https://help.manus.im/en/)

[Billing](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/13760762-billing)

[Credits & Usage](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/15919440-credits-usage)

What are the rules for credits consumption? And how can I obtain them?

What are the rules for credits consumption? And how can I obtain them?
======================================================================

Learn how Manus credits work, consumption rules, and how to obtain more credits.

Updated this week

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711097-what-are-the-rules-for-credits-consumption-and-how-can-i-obtain-them#h_a43da6039d)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711097-what-are-the-rules-for-credits-consumption-and-how-can-i-obtain-them#h_7b459051ff)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711097-what-are-the-rules-for-credits-consumption-and-how-can-i-obtain-them#h_3dbe093a6a)

How do credits work?
====================

Credits are primarily consumed based on:

*   **LLM tokens**: Used for task planning, decision making, and output generation.
    
*   **Virtual machines**: Used for cloud environments that support file operations, browser automation, and code execution.
    
*   **Third-party APIs**: Used for accessing integrated external services, such as financial data and professional databases.
    

The specific credits consumption for a task is determined by its complexity and duration. Credits are only consumed during active task processing. Completed tasks and the storage or deployment of their outputs do not consume any credits, so there's no need to delete completed tasks.

We provide a full refund of consumed credits for tasks that fail due to technical issues on our end. We will continuously optimize system efficiency and reduce the number of credits consumed per task.

How to get more credits?
========================

*   For Free users, you can upgrade to a Pro membership for more credits.
    
*   Members who need additional credits can switch to a higher plan.
    

To learn more about membership benefits or to upgrade to a paid plan, **[click here.](https://manus.ai/pricing)
**

Will credits expire?
====================

*   Credits are consumed in the following order: event credits > daily credits > monthly credits > add-on credits > free credits.
    
*   The monthly consumption limit for daily refresh credits for free users is set to 1,500 credits; paid users have no limit. Daily credits can only be used for Manus 1.6 lite.
    
*   Monthly credits are obtained through subscription and automatically refresh on the same date each month based on your subscription date.
    
*   Free credits never expire.
    
*   Unused credits require an active paid subscription to remain valid. If your subscription is canceled, any remaining purchased credits may no longer be accessible.
    
*   Event credits can be earned by participating in events and expire when the event ends.
    
*   Monthly credits need to be used within the subscription period. For example, if you purchase a $20 Pro membership on January 1st, you will receive 4000 monthly credits, and these credits need to be used before February 1st. If not used up, they will reset on February 1st.
    

Common related FAQs:

*   How do credits work?
    
*   What determines how many credits a task will consume?
    
*   Do completed tasks consume credits?
    
*   How can I get more credits as a Free user?
    
*   Will credits expire?
    
*   In what order are the credits types consumed?
    
*   What happens if a task fails due to technical issues?
    
*   How often and when do monthly credits refresh?
    

* * *

¿Qué sucede con mis créditos después de cancelar o dejar que mi suscripción a Manus expire?

¿Qué sucede con mis créditos después de cancelar o dejar que mi suscripción a Manus expire?
===========================================================================================

Aprenda qué sucede con sus créditos de Manus cuando cancela o deja que su suscripción expire.

Actualizado hace más de 3 semanas

Índice de contenidos

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/12268225-que-sucede-con-mis-creditos-despues-de-cancelar-o-dejar-que-mi-suscripcion-a-manus-expire#h_b30244554f)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/12268225-que-sucede-con-mis-creditos-despues-de-cancelar-o-dejar-que-mi-suscripcion-a-manus-expire#h_8e76a52932)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/12268225-que-sucede-con-mis-creditos-despues-de-cancelar-o-dejar-que-mi-suscripcion-a-manus-expire#h_f558c01150)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/12268225-que-sucede-con-mis-creditos-despues-de-cancelar-o-dejar-que-mi-suscripcion-a-manus-expire#h_f0cdae07b1)

Comprender qué sucede con sus créditos después de cancelar o dejar que su suscripción a Manus expire es esencial para aprovechar al máximo los beneficios de su membresía. Aquí tiene una guía detallada:

Impacto de la Cancelación de la Suscripción en los Créditos
===========================================================

Cuando su suscripción a Manus se cancela o expira, ocurre lo siguiente:

*   Todos los beneficios de la membresía, incluido el acceso a los créditos, finalizan tan pronto como termina la suscripción.
    
*   Cualquier crédito no utilizado restante de las asignaciones mensuales se restablece a 0 una vez que finaliza el ciclo de suscripción.
    
*   Para los usuarios con una prueba gratuita de siete días, si cancela su suscripción antes del cargo, no se incurrirá en ningún cargo. Si cancela su suscripción después de que se le haya cobrado, no habrá reembolso y solo se cancelará la próxima renovación.
    

Uso de Créditos Mensuales y de Eventos
======================================

*   **Créditos Mensuales**: Estos están directamente vinculados a su suscripción activa. Una vez que su suscripción expire, cualquier crédito mensual restante dejará de estar disponible.
    
*   **Créditos de Eventos**: Estos créditos solo se pueden usar con una suscripción de pago activa. Si su cuenta cambia a una membresía Free o la suscripción caduca, estos créditos se vuelven inactivos.
    

Reactivación de Créditos Después de la Renovación de la Suscripción
===================================================================

Si renueva su suscripción o se suscribe a un nuevo plan de membresía, los créditos no utilizados previamente pueden reactivarse. Sin embargo, los créditos mensuales que se restablecieron a 0 no se pueden recuperar.

Recomendaciones para el Uso de Créditos
=======================================

Para evitar perder créditos, se recomienda encarecidamente:

*   Utilizar todos los créditos comprados dentro de su ciclo de suscripción.
    
*   Planificar el uso de créditos con anticipación, especialmente si prevé cancelar su suscripción o cambiar a una membresía Free.
    

Al comprender y seguir estas pautas, puede hacer un uso efectivo de sus créditos y evitar su desactivación.

Preguntas frecuentes relacionadas comunes:

*   ¿Qué sucede con mis créditos mensuales cuando mi suscripción expira?
    
*   ¿Qué sucede con mis créditos de eventos después de la cancelación?
    
*   ¿Puedo reactivar mis créditos si renuevo mi suscripción?
    
*   ¿Se pueden recuperar los créditos mensuales después de la renovación?
    
*   ¿Cómo puedo evitar perder mis créditos?
    
*   ¿Cuándo finalizan los beneficios de mi membresía después de la cancelación/terminación?
    
*   ¿Qué debo hacer si planeo cancelar mi suscripción?
    
*   ¿Se restablecen los créditos mensuales no utilizados cuando finaliza la suscripción?

# ¿Cómo optimizar mi uso de créditos? | Manus Help Center

[Ir al contenido principal](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/12087847-como-optimizar-mi-uso-de-creditos#main-content)

Índice de contenidos

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/12087847-como-optimizar-mi-uso-de-creditos#h_c0f911a20d)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/12087847-como-optimizar-mi-uso-de-creditos#h_9a5878f5a9)

¿Cómo optimizar mi uso de créditos?

¿Cómo optimizar mi uso de créditos?
===================================

Aprenda estrategias efectivas para optimizar su uso de créditos de Manus.

Actualizado hace más de 3 semanas

Índice de contenidos

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/12087847-como-optimizar-mi-uso-de-creditos#h_c0f911a20d)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/12087847-como-optimizar-mi-uso-de-creditos#h_9a5878f5a9)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/12087847-como-optimizar-mi-uso-de-creditos#h_ac7cd8f3e0)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/12087847-como-optimizar-mi-uso-de-creditos#h_02f3983ca3)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/12087847-como-optimizar-mi-uso-de-creditos#h_0ab3828894)

Al usar Manus, la gestión de créditos es esencial. A continuación, se presentan estrategias clave para ayudarle a optimizar su uso de créditos de manera efectiva.

Estrategias para Optimizar el Uso de Créditos
=============================================

1\. Combine Preguntas Similares
-------------------------------

Siempre que sea posible, agrupe preguntas relacionadas o similares en una sola tarea. Al hacerlo:

*   Puede reducir el número de intentos separados que consumen créditos.
    
*   La agrupación optimizada permite una resolución consolidada y eficiente.
    

Ejemplo: En lugar de hacer preguntas separadas sobre cómo formatear y guardar un archivo, combínelas en una sola consulta integral.

2\. Agilice las Instrucciones
-----------------------------

Proporcione instrucciones claras, concisas y directas al interactuar con Manus. Las estrategias incluyen:

*   Indicar claramente sus expectativas o resultados en un solo paso en lugar de múltiples instrucciones vagas.
    
*   Evitar la elaboración innecesaria o el fraseo duplicado.
    

Ejemplo: En lugar de preguntar: "¿Puedes ayudarme a crear un informe? Necesito una lista, ¿y también puede incluir gráficos?", agilice con: "Cree un informe con una lista y gráficos."

3\. Reduzca los Intentos Repetidos
----------------------------------

Hacer repetidamente variaciones de la misma pregunta puede agotar los créditos innecesariamente. En su lugar:

*   Revise cuidadosamente las respuestas proporcionadas antes de volver a enviar consultas similares.
    
*   Realice correcciones a sus entradas o instrucciones para obtener mejores tasas de éxito.
    

Ejemplo: Si una pregunta no produce la respuesta deseada, refínela basándose en la respuesta inicial en lugar de reformularla sin rumbo.

Beneficios del Uso Optimizado de Créditos
=========================================

Al implementar estas estrategias, los usuarios pueden:

*   Maximizar la eficiencia con su asignación actual de créditos.
    
*   Experimentar flujos de trabajo más fluidos y una finalización de tareas más rápida.
    

Adherirse a estas prácticas garantiza que obtenga el máximo provecho de Manus. Planificar proactivamente sus preguntas y refinar cómo interactúa con la plataforma puede mejorar significativamente su experiencia de uso de créditos.

Preguntas frecuentes relacionadas comunes:

*   ¿Cómo puede ayudar la combinación de preguntas similares a optimizar el uso de créditos?
    
*   ¿Cómo puedo reducir los intentos repetidos?
    
*   ¿Cuáles son los beneficios del uso optimizado de créditos?
    
*   ¿Por qué es esencial la gestión de créditos al usar Manus?
    
*   ¿Cómo puedo maximizar la eficiencia con mi asignación actual de créditos?
    
*   ¿Cómo puede la planificación proactiva mejorar el uso de créditos?
    

* * *

¿Cuál es el precio actual de la membresía de Manus?

¿Cuál es el precio actual de la membresía de Manus?
===================================================

Obtenga información sobre los planes mensuales y anuales, las ubicaciones de precios y cuánto puede ahorrar con las suscripciones anuales.

Actualizado hace más de una semana

Índice de contenidos

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711111-cual-es-el-precio-actual-de-la-membresia-de-manus#h_c9bdaff16f)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711111-cual-es-el-precio-actual-de-la-membresia-de-manus#h_38148d742d)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711111-cual-es-el-precio-actual-de-la-membresia-de-manus#h_21fb3f149c)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711111-cual-es-el-precio-actual-de-la-membresia-de-manus#h_f03f04c213)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711111-cual-es-el-precio-actual-de-la-membresia-de-manus#h_85ce5f4585)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711111-cual-es-el-precio-actual-de-la-membresia-de-manus#h_2cc25c261a)

Puede encontrar nuestros precios a través de [manus.im/home](http://manus.im/home)
 -> [https://manus.im/pricing](https://manus.im/pricing)
.

Después de ingresar a la página de inicio de Manus, desplácese hasta la parte inferior de la página para ver el precio de nuestros productos.

Actualmente, Manus ofrece opciones de planes Free & Pro & Team para satisfacer las necesidades de diferentes usuarios. Ya sea un usuario individual o un usuario Team, Manus puede proporcionarle soluciones eficientes.

**_\*Tenga en cuenta que los usuarios Free solo tienen acceso a Manus 1.6 Lite en Modo Agent, mientras que los usuarios Pro tienen acceso a Manus 1.6, Manus 1.6 Max y Manus 1.6 Lite. Tanto los usuarios Free como Pro tienen acceso a Modo Chat._**

Aquí están los contenidos detallados de cada plan:

【Precio del Plan Free: $0/mes】
==============================

1.  Acceso a Modo Chat y Manus 1.6 Lite en Modo Agent.
    
2.  Características: Créditos de Actualización Diaria: 300 créditos proporcionados diariamente para responder rápidamente preguntas sencillas.
    
3.  Tareas Concurrentes: Admite 1 tarea concurrente.
    
4.  Tareas Programadas: Admite 2 tareas programadas.
    
5.  Casos de Uso: Adecuado para usuarios individuales con bajos requisitos funcionales para experimentar las características básicas de Manus.
    

【Precio del Plan Pro: A partir de $20/mes (Disfrute de un 17% de descuento con facturación anual)】
==================================================================================================

Los usuarios Free pueden actualizar a una membresía para obtener más créditos. Los miembros que necesiten créditos adicionales pueden cambiar a un plan superior.

1.  Acceso a Modo Chat y Manus 1.6 Max, Manus 1.6 y Manus 1.6 Lite en Modo Agent.
    
2.  Características: Créditos Mensuales: A partir de 4,000 créditos por mes, lo que soporta necesidades de uso de mayor frecuencia.
    
3.  Investigación Avanzada: Admite investigación avanzada sobre cualquier tema.
    
4.  Implementación Profesional de Sitios Web: Proporciona servicios de implementación de sitios web de nivel profesional.
    
5.  Generación de Diapositivas: Genera diapositivas con conocimientos profundos y una estructura clara.
    
6.  Investigación Amplia: Rinde mejor en tareas de alta intensidad.
    
7.  Cantidad de Tareas: Admite 20 tareas concurrentes y 20 tareas programadas.
    
8.  Acceso Anticipado a Funciones Beta: Experimente las últimas funciones por adelantado.
    
9.  Casos de Uso: Adecuado para usuarios que necesitan realizar investigaciones en profundidad y generar informes profesionales, ayudando a mejorar la eficiencia del trabajo.
    

【Precio del Plan Team: A partir de $40 por asiento/mes (Disfrute de un 17% de descuento con facturación anual)】
===============================================================================================================

1.  Acceso a Modo Chat y Manus 1.6 Max, Manus 1.6 y Manus 1.6 Lite en modo Agent.
    
2.  Usuarios Objetivo: Usuarios Team que necesitan colaboración y funciones de gestión avanzadas.
    
3.  Características: Incluye todas las funciones del plan Pro.
    
4.  SSO (Inicio de Sesión Único): Proporciona métodos de inicio de sesión más convenientes.
    
5.  Exclusión Voluntaria del Entrenamiento de Datos: Admite la exclusión voluntaria del entrenamiento de datos para proteger la privacidad.
    
6.  Análisis de Uso de Team: Proporciona datos analíticos sobre el uso del Team.
    
7.  Control de Acceso Interno: Mejor gestión de los permisos del equipo.
    
8.  Plantillas de Diapositivas Compartidas: Proporciona plantillas de diapositivas compartidas para que los equipos mejoren la eficiencia de la colaboración.
    
9.  Casos de Uso: Adecuado para usuarios empresariales o Team que necesitan colaboración en equipo, protección de la privacidad de los datos y funciones de gestión avanzadas.
    

Todo está sujeto a lo que se muestra en la página de precios real.

-------------

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1889672090/8e877150bb7953db969bd6276081/image.png?expires=1766962800&signature=8cecce8eea350b4ab90951dc6d6d73da651e685d6c804446ea5c1e72410015cf&req=dSgvH895n4FWWfMW1HO4zf8dQEQyP%2B3XnijnxFAGxK9v%2BVA2T1F%2FKSCeg2D2%0AZF%2BkNyzKp4cJm9z83go%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1889672090/8e877150bb7953db969bd6276081/image.png?expires=1766962800&signature=8cecce8eea350b4ab90951dc6d6d73da651e685d6c804446ea5c1e72410015cf&req=dSgvH895n4FWWfMW1HO4zf8dQEQyP%2B3XnijnxFAGxK9v%2BVA2T1F%2FKSCeg2D2%0AZF%2BkNyzKp4cJm9z83go%3D%0A)

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1889672497/8b0218f344d55af3dc295dcffb0d/image.png?expires=1766962800&signature=38412bb3cd66a72d133b1d94e70b5ad5b3ba806f221e73c89b48f980dccd3b15&req=dSgvH895n4VWXvMW1HO4zV%2ByiVuPQ9PsganfhkBJ21yz2iNlCz3PySSbE8RI%0A04e6q4Whp4WrfZrYfGw%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1889672497/8b0218f344d55af3dc295dcffb0d/image.png?expires=1766962800&signature=38412bb3cd66a72d133b1d94e70b5ad5b3ba806f221e73c89b48f980dccd3b15&req=dSgvH895n4VWXvMW1HO4zV%2ByiVuPQ9PsganfhkBJ21yz2iNlCz3PySSbE8RI%0A04e6q4Whp4WrfZrYfGw%3D%0A)

Solución de problemas:
======================

Pregunta: ¿Qué pasará con los miembros existentes bajo los nuevos planes de precios?

*   Los usuarios miembros existentes seguirán renovándose automáticamente con precios sin cambios y podrán actualizar o degradar a nuevos planes. Los planes originales Basic y Plus han sido renombrados a Pro.

# ¿Dónde puedo verificar mi consumo/uso de créditos? | Manus Help Center

¿Dónde puedo verificar mi consumo/uso de créditos?

¿Dónde puedo verificar mi consumo/uso de créditos?
==================================================

Vea su historial completo de uso de créditos, detalles de transacciones y cambios de saldo.

Actualizado hace más de una semana

**Nuestro Compromiso con el Uso Transparente de Créditos**

Comprender cómo se utilizan sus créditos es esencial para maximizar el valor de su suscripción a Manus. Creemos en la transparencia total, por lo que proporcionamos una página de uso de créditos detallada y fácil de entender. Este panel le permite rastrear cada transacción de créditos, desde compras y renovaciones mensuales hasta el consumo individual de tareas, dándole control total sobre su cuenta.

Esta guía le explicará cómo acceder a su historial de uso, qué significa la información y qué hacer si tiene alguna pregunta sobre una transacción específica.

**Acceso a su Panel de Uso de Créditos**

Puede visitar su Settings > Usage para ver cómo se consumieron/utilizaron sus créditos, así como la fecha, los detalles de la transacción y el cambio en los créditos.

Puede consultar las siguientes capturas de pantalla para obtener orientación:

What can I do if my temporary deployment link has expired?

What can I do if my temporary deployment link has expired?
==========================================================

Learn what to do when your Manus temporary deployment link expires.

Updated over 2 weeks ago

The temporary deployment feature of Manus typically generates links that include the "manus.computer" domain. These temporary deployment sites usually have a short lifespan. Temporary links in the sandbox are for testing purposes only and will become unavailable during the hibernation period. We will continuously improve this experience in future version updates. You can choose to use the permanent deployment feature to obtain the desired results.

# ¿Cuál es la unidad de precio de Manus a nivel global? ¿Puedo pagar en moneda local? | Manus Help Center

[Ir al contenido principal](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711125-cual-es-la-unidad-de-precio-de-manus-a-nivel-global-puedo-pagar-en-moneda-local#main-content)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711125-cual-es-la-unidad-de-precio-de-manus-a-nivel-global-puedo-pagar-en-moneda-local#h_58f7e0101a)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711125-cual-es-la-unidad-de-precio-de-manus-a-nivel-global-puedo-pagar-en-moneda-local#h_b6b08948e1)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711125-cual-es-la-unidad-de-precio-de-manus-a-nivel-global-puedo-pagar-en-moneda-local#h_f050441626)

[Todas las colecciones](https://help.manus.im/es/)

[Facturación](http://help.manus.im/es/collections/13760762-facturacion)

[Precios & Planes](http://help.manus.im/es/collections/15919468-precios-planes)

¿Cuál es la unidad de precio de Manus a nivel global? ¿Puedo pagar en moneda local?

¿Cuál es la unidad de precio de Manus a nivel global? ¿Puedo pagar en moneda local?
===================================================================================

Obtenga información sobre los precios globales de Manus en USD y las opciones de pago en moneda local.

Actualizado esta semana

Índice de contenidos

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711125-cual-es-la-unidad-de-precio-de-manus-a-nivel-global-puedo-pagar-en-moneda-local#h_58f7e0101a)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711125-cual-es-la-unidad-de-precio-de-manus-a-nivel-global-puedo-pagar-en-moneda-local#h_b6b08948e1)

[](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711125-cual-es-la-unidad-de-precio-de-manus-a-nivel-global-puedo-pagar-en-moneda-local#h_f050441626)

Nuestro compromiso con precios globales justos y transparentes
==============================================================

Para servir a nuestra comunidad global de manera efectiva, Manus ha establecido una estructura de precios clara y consistente. Entendemos que la gestión de pagos internacionales a veces puede ser compleja, y nos comprometemos a hacer que el proceso sea lo más transparente posible. Todos nuestros precios de suscripción y créditos están estandarizados en Dólares de los Estados Unidos (USD) para garantizar la equidad e igualdad para todos los usuarios, independientemente de su ubicación.

Esta guía explica por qué utilizamos el USD como nuestra unidad de precio, cómo puede pagar en su moneda local y qué esperar con respecto a los tipos de cambio y las posibles tarifas.

Cómo funciona el pago en su moneda local
========================================

Aunque nuestros precios están listados en USD, usted puede pagar absolutamente utilizando su moneda local. El proceso de conversión es manejado automáticamente por su institución financiera en el punto de venta. Aquí tiene un desglose claro de quién maneja qué en el proceso de transacción:

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Entidad | Función y Responsabilidad |
| **Manus** | Establece el precio base del producto en USD. Por ejemplo, un plan de suscripción podría estar listado como $20 USD. Esta es la cantidad que cobra Manus. |
| **Su Banco o Proveedor de Pagos**  <br>(ej., Visa, Mastercard, PayPal) | 1\. Convierte el precio en USD a su moneda local.<br><br>2\. Determina el tipo de cambio utilizado para esta conversión.<br><br>3\. Aplica cualquier tarifa relevante, como tarifas de conversión de moneda o tarifas de transacción extranjera.<br><br>4\. Le cobra la cantidad final convertida en su moneda local. |
|     |     |

**_\*En resumen: Manus establece el precio en USD, y su banco determina la cantidad final que usted paga en su moneda local._**

Comprensión de posibles cargos adicionales
==========================================

La cantidad final que se le cobra puede ser ligeramente diferente de una conversión directa del precio en USD que ve en línea. Esto se debe a las tarifas cobradas por su banco, no por Manus.

*   Tarifas de Conversión de Moneda: Muchos bancos cobran una pequeña tarifa porcentual por convertir una moneda a otra. Esta es una práctica estándar para las transacciones internacionales.
    
*   Tarifas de Transacción Extranjera: Algunos emisores de tarjetas añaden un recargo por cualquier compra procesada por un comerciante en otro país.
    

Para evitar sorpresas, le recomendamos encarecidamente que se ponga en contacto con su banco o proveedor de tarjetas antes de realizar una compra para preguntar sobre sus políticas y tarifas específicas para transacciones internacionales en USD.

Preguntas frecuentes relacionadas:

*   ¿Se muestran los precios en mi moneda local?
    
*   ¿Cómo se gestiona la conversión de moneda?
    
*   ¿Se me cobrarán tarifas de conversión de moneda?
    
*   ¿De qué debo estar al tanto antes de realizar un pago?
    
*   ¿Quién determina la cantidad final cobrada?
    

* * *

# What should I do if my daily credits have not refreshed? | Manus Help Center

[Skip to main content](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11985189-what-should-i-do-if-my-daily-credits-have-not-refreshed#main-content)

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11985189-what-should-i-do-if-my-daily-credits-have-not-refreshed#h_77d4862b91)

[Credits & Usage](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/15919440-credits-usage)

What should I do if my daily credits have not refreshed?

What should I do if my daily credits have not refreshed?
========================================================

Troubleshoot daily credit refresh issues on Manus.

Updated over a week ago

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11985189-what-should-i-do-if-my-daily-credits-have-not-refreshed#h_77d4862b91)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11985189-what-should-i-do-if-my-daily-credits-have-not-refreshed#h_50f3db5df4)

**Understanding the Daily Credit Refresh Process**
--------------------------------------------------

We understand it can be concerning when you log in expecting your 300 daily refresh credits and don't see them. These credits reward you for being an active member of the Manus community, and we want to ensure you receive them reliably.

Regarding daily credits, you need to log in to Manus every day to claim 300 free credits. Please note that credit refresh may experience slight delays. The 300 daily credits are only valid for that day and will reset the next day; they will not accumulate in your account balance.

\***_Please note that Free users have a daily refreshed free credit usage limit of 1,500 credits per month. After reaching 1,500 credits, daily free credits will no longer refresh._**

Usually, when daily credits appear to be missing, it is due to one of a few common reasons related to timing, usage limits for free accounts, or how credits are displayed. This guide provides a step-by-step process to help you troubleshoot the issue and understand what to do if the problem persists.

Why Credits May Seem to Be Missing
----------------------------------

Since daily credits have a higher priority in the consumption order of different credit types, it's possible that your daily credits were consumed during the process of executing a task. Please note that, as a refresh-based credit type, the increase and decrease details of daily credits will not be displayed on the 'Details' homepage of the 'Usage' interface.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1792389780/1c1c4e22e76d062a91706dd7503a/image.png?expires=1766961900&signature=cd858a0dfbbac576e19691b1224974be03abf3d5ecc3af41751f721611429b4f&req=dScuFMp2lIZXWfMW1HO4zaQkMq97oHXMn7BJ6IES8wTJ8ivxWbholK3pSZPz%0ARGcndpm6l0Li3mnNXNA%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1792389780/1c1c4e22e76d062a91706dd7503a/image.png?expires=1766961900&signature=cd858a0dfbbac576e19691b1224974be03abf3d5ecc3af41751f721611429b4f&req=dScuFMp2lIZXWfMW1HO4zaQkMq97oHXMn7BJ6IES8wTJ8ivxWbholK3pSZPz%0ARGcndpm6l0Li3mnNXNA%3D%0A)

If you are certain that the daily credits have not been credited to your account, you can take a screenshot of your credit details interface after the credit refresh time on a certain day, before initiating any conversation, and send it to us.

Please make sure to include the real-time system clock, and we will investigate the issue for you.

Common related FAQs:

*   How do I claim my daily credits?
    
*   Why might my daily credits not appear?
    
*   Will my daily credits show up in the usage details?
    
*   What should I do if I'm certain my daily credits were not credited?
    
*   Can there be delays in credit refresh?

Solución de problemas & Limitaciones
====================================

# How can I share a task? | Manus Help Center

[Skip to main content](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711198-how-can-i-share-a-task#main-content)

[All Collections](https://help.manus.im/en/)

[Feature](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/13762621-feature)

[Task & Environment Management](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/15921567-task-environment-management)

How can I share a task?

How can I share a task?
=======================

Share public task links with the support team, family, or friends in 4 easy steps for better assistance and collaboration.

Updated over a week ago

If users encounter any difficulties during their task with Manus or need assistance from the support team, they can share the public task link with the support team to get help. This is not mandatory, but having the task link allows the support team to provide more targeted suggestions and assistance.

Therefore, to better understand the conversation scenario for problem identification and troubleshooting, it is suggested to share the public task link by:

1.  Click the share button in the top right area of the task.
    
2.  Click the public access button.
    
3.  Click the copy link button.
    
4.  Send us the public access task link.
    

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1889491644/4dfae8553b9183f16a712af70443/image.png?expires=1766961900&signature=e44068f5d32fb3d5f36d68c9d60c7ab9ac601fb7084bd8a91d8b8c4dce1bc055&req=dSgvH813nIdbXfMW1HO4zcqxUyj8y1YfZQVwstMcHFr9dBjT9%2B%2BHr%2FVlII0K%0AClg2KzeG5ZneD7q3Cts%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1889491644/4dfae8553b9183f16a712af70443/image.png?expires=1766961900&signature=e44068f5d32fb3d5f36d68c9d60c7ab9ac601fb7084bd8a91d8b8c4dce1bc055&req=dSgvH813nIdbXfMW1HO4zcqxUyj8y1YfZQVwstMcHFr9dBjT9%2B%2BHr%2FVlII0K%0AClg2KzeG5ZneD7q3Cts%3D%0A)

Besides, users can also share their tasks with their family or friends in this way, showcasing their usage process and experience with them.

Where can I check my credit consumption/usage?

Where can I check my credit consumption/usage?
==============================================

View your complete credit usage history, transaction details, and balance changes.

Updated over a week ago

**Our Commitment to Transparent Credit Usage**

Understanding how your credits are used is essential for maximizing the value of your Manus subscription. We believe in complete transparency, which is why we provide a detailed and easy-to-understand credit usage page. This dashboard allows you to track every credit transaction, from purchases and monthly renewals to individual task consumption, giving you full control over your account.

This guide will walk you through how to access your usage history, what the information means, and what to do if you have any questions about a specific transaction.

**Accessing Your Credit Usage Dashboard**

You may visit your Settings > Usage to view how your credits were being consumed/used, as well as the date, transaction details, and the change in credits.

You may refer to the following screenshots for guidance:

How can I take over Manus' browser or VS code?
==============================================

Take manual control over Manus' browser when it needs assistance or when you want to intervene in tasks.

Updated over a week ago

When Manus encounters difficulties while performing tasks and needs assistance, or when the user wishes to intervene manually, the user can take control of Manus's computer, operating the browser or VS Code to help Manus overcome certain challenges in the tasks. Manus will prompt users to take over when it requires assistance from them.

# How to optimize my credit usage? | Manus Help Center

[Credits & Usage](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/15919440-credits-usage)

How to optimize my credit usage?

How to optimize my credit usage?
================================

Learn effective strategies to optimize your Manus credit usage.

Updated over 3 weeks ago

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12087847-how-to-optimize-my-credit-usage#h_c0f911a20d)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12087847-how-to-optimize-my-credit-usage#h_9a5878f5a9)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12087847-how-to-optimize-my-credit-usage#h_ac7cd8f3e0)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12087847-how-to-optimize-my-credit-usage#h_02f3983ca3)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12087847-how-to-optimize-my-credit-usage#h_0ab3828894)

When using Manus, credit management is essential. Below are key strategies to help you optimize your credit usage effectively.

Strategies to Optimize Credit Usage
===================================

1\. Combine Similar Questions
-----------------------------

Whenever possible, group related or similar questions into one task. By doing so:

*   You can reduce the number of separate attempts that consume credits.
    
*   Streamlined grouping allows for consolidated and efficient resolution.
    

Example: Instead of asking separate questions about formatting and saving a file, combine them into one comprehensive query.

2\. Streamline Instructions
---------------------------

Provide clear, concise, and direct instructions when engaging Manus. Strategies include:

*   Clearly stating your expectations or outcomes in one step instead of multiple vague instructions.
    
*   Avoiding unnecessary elaboration or duplicate phrasing.
    

Example: Instead of asking, "Can you help create a report? I need a list, and can it also include charts?” streamline with, "Create a report with both a list and charts."

3\. Reduce Repeated Attempts
----------------------------

Repeatedly asking variations of the same question can exhaust credits unnecessarily. Instead:

*   Review the responses provided carefully before resubmitting similar queries.
    
*   Make corrections to your inputs or instructions for better success rates.
    

Example: If a question does not yield the intended answer, refine it based on the initial response instead of rephrasing aimlessly.

Benefits of Optimized Credit Usage
==================================

By implementing these strategies, users can:

*   Maximize efficiency with their current credit allocation.
    
*   Experience smoother workflows and faster task completion.
    

Adhering to these practices ensures you get the most from Manus. Proactively planning your questions and refining how you interact with the platform can significantly improve your credit usage experience.

Common related FAQs:

*   How can combining similar questions help optimize credit usage?
    
*   How can I reduce repeated attempts?
    
*   What are the benefits of optimized credit usage?
    
*   Why is credit management essential when using Manus?
    
*   How can I maximize efficiency with my current credit allocation?
    
*   How can proactive planning improve credit usage?

# What is the pricing unit for Manus globally? Can I pay in local currency? | Manus Help Center

[Skip to main content](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711125-what-is-the-pricing-unit-for-manus-globally-can-i-pay-in-local-currency#main-content)

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711125-what-is-the-pricing-unit-for-manus-globally-can-i-pay-in-local-currency#h_58f7e0101a)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711125-what-is-the-pricing-unit-for-manus-globally-can-i-pay-in-local-currency#h_b6b08948e1)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711125-what-is-the-pricing-unit-for-manus-globally-can-i-pay-in-local-currency#h_f050441626)

[All Collections](https://help.manus.im/en/)

[Billing](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/13760762-billing)

[Pricing & Plans](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/15919468-pricing-plans)

What is the pricing unit for Manus globally? Can I pay in local currency?

What is the pricing unit for Manus globally? Can I pay in local currency?
=========================================================================

Learn about Manus global pricing in USD and local currency payment options.

Updated this week

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711125-what-is-the-pricing-unit-for-manus-globally-can-i-pay-in-local-currency#h_58f7e0101a)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711125-what-is-the-pricing-unit-for-manus-globally-can-i-pay-in-local-currency#h_b6b08948e1)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711125-what-is-the-pricing-unit-for-manus-globally-can-i-pay-in-local-currency#h_f050441626)

**Our Commitment to Fair and Transparent Global Pricing**
---------------------------------------------------------

To serve our global community effectively, Manus has established a clear and consistent pricing structure. We understand that navigating international payments can sometimes be complex, and we are committed to making the process as transparent as possible. All our subscription and credit prices are standardized in United States Dollars (USD) to ensure fairness and equality for all users, regardless of their location.

This guide explains why we use USD as our pricing unit, how you can pay in your local currency, and what to expect regarding exchange rates and potential fees.

**How Paying in Your Local Currency Works**
-------------------------------------------

While our prices are listed in USD, you can absolutely pay using your local currency. The conversion process is handled automatically by your financial institution at the point of sale. Here is a clear breakdown of who handles what in the transaction process:

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Entity | Role and Responsibility |
| **Manus** | Sets the base price of the product in USD. For example, a subscription plan might be listed as $20 USD. This is the amount that Manus charges. |
| **Your Bank or Payment Provider**  <br>(e.g., Visa, Mastercard, PayPal) | 1\. Converts the USD price to your local currency.<br><br>2\. Determines the exchange rate used for this conversion.<br><br>3\. Applies any relevant fees, such as currency conversion or foreign transaction fees.<br><br>4\. Charges you the final, converted amount in your local currency. |
|     |     |

**_\*In short: Manus sets the USD price, and your bank determines the final amount you pay in your local currency._**

**Understanding Potential Additional Charges**
----------------------------------------------

The final amount you are charged may be slightly different from a direct conversion of the USD price you see online. This is due to fees charged by your bank, not by Manus.

*   Currency Conversion Fees: Many banks charge a small percentage fee for converting one currency to another. This is a standard practice for international transactions.
    
*   Foreign Transaction Fees: Some card issuers add a surcharge for any purchase that is processed by a merchant in another country.
    

To avoid surprises, we strongly recommend that you contact your bank or card provider before making a purchase to ask about their specific policies and fees for international transactions in USD.

Common related FAQs:

*   Are prices shown in my local currency?
    
*   How is the currency conversion handled?
    
*   Will I be charged currency conversion fees?
    
*   What should I be aware of before making a payment?
    
*   Who determines the final charged amount?
    

* * *

# ¿Cómo puedo compartir una tarea? | Manus Help Center

[Ir al contenido principal](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711198-como-puedo-compartir-una-tarea#main-content)

[Todas las colecciones](https://help.manus.im/es/)

[Función](http://help.manus.im/es/collections/13762621-funcion)

[Gestión de Tareas & Entorno](http://help.manus.im/es/collections/15921567-gestion-de-tareas-entorno)

¿Cómo puedo compartir una tarea?

¿Cómo puedo compartir una tarea?
================================

Actualizado hace más de una semana

Si los usuarios encuentran alguna dificultad durante su tarea con Manus o necesitan asistencia del equipo de soporte, pueden compartir el enlace de la tarea pública con el equipo de soporte para obtener ayuda. Esto no es obligatorio, pero tener el enlace de la tarea permite al equipo de soporte proporcionar sugerencias y asistencia más específicas.

Por lo tanto, para comprender mejor el escenario de la conversación para la identificación y solución de problemas, se sugiere compartir el enlace de la tarea pública mediante:

1.  Haz clic en el botón de compartir en la esquina superior derecha de la tarea.
    
2.  Haz clic en el botón de acceso público.
    
3.  Haz clic en el botón de copiar enlace.
    
4.  Envíanos el enlace de la tarea de acceso público.
    

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1889491644/4dfae8553b9183f16a712af70443/image.png?expires=1766962800&signature=9793b6016ba23bb26559bd6725cabb1affc4528ff3ac102c186e7aa3368b6675&req=dSgvH813nIdbXfMW1HO4zcqxUyj8y1UeZQVwstMcHFpLCIz80msyv2YwJYSb%0A%2BCxBeULxBvEBdv%2FEWfg%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1889491644/4dfae8553b9183f16a712af70443/image.png?expires=1766962800&signature=9793b6016ba23bb26559bd6725cabb1affc4528ff3ac102c186e7aa3368b6675&req=dSgvH813nIdbXfMW1HO4zcqxUyj8y1UeZQVwstMcHFpLCIz80msyv2YwJYSb%0A%2BCxBeULxBvEBdv%2FEWfg%3D%0A)

Además, los usuarios también pueden compartir sus tareas con sus familiares o amigos de esta manera, mostrando su proceso de uso y experiencia con ellos.

What can I do if I encounter a sandbox issue in the task?

What can I do if I encounter a sandbox issue in the task?
=========================================================

Learn how to handle sandbox errors in Manus. Restart the sandbox to continue your task without losing progress.

Updated over 2 weeks ago

Currently, we provide the following tip for sandbox errors encountered during a task to help users restart the sandbox and continue the task. Resetting the sandbox will not reset task progress. If you do not see this tip or if task progress is lost after resetting the sandbox, please contact us.

# ¿Qué puedo hacer si encuentro un error interno del servidor (10091)? | Manus Help Center

[Ir al contenido principal](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711263-que-puedo-hacer-si-encuentro-un-error-interno-del-servidor-10091#main-content)

[Todas las colecciones](https://help.manus.im/es/)

[Función](http://help.manus.im/es/collections/13762621-funcion)

[Solución de problemas & Limitaciones](http://help.manus.im/es/collections/15921659-solucion-de-problemas-limitaciones)

¿Qué puedo hacer si encuentro un error interno del servidor (10091)?

¿Qué puedo hacer si encuentro un error interno del servidor (10091)?
====================================================================

Aprende a manejar el error 10091 en Manus.

Actualizado hace más de 2 semanas

Actualmente, proporcionamos este consejo a los usuarios cuyas tareas se terminan debido a una carga alta, permitiéndoles elegir si continuar o detenerse y recibir un reembolso de créditos.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1603178045/3c0c52fc7434c21f379df6a3af5f/asynccode?expires=1766962800&signature=4833c7a691e529d627b9b76bb2a4356d9f77a6309baf17b770a935e8cc9efbe9&req=dSYnFch5lYFbXPMW1HO4zXzEOi7vrzA196vd0DV%2Bx9q1f8SlNOk5unNSoR0H%0Apnl18HCzuTkiDdKQZPo%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1603178045/3c0c52fc7434c21f379df6a3af5f/asynccode?expires=1766962800&signature=4833c7a691e529d627b9b76bb2a4356d9f77a6309baf17b770a935e8cc9efbe9&req=dSYnFch5lYFbXPMW1HO4zXzEOi7vrzA196vd0DV%2Bx9q1f8SlNOk5unNSoR0H%0Apnl18HCzuTkiDdKQZPo%3D%0A)

Este error ocurre generalmente cuando hay un alto volumen de acceso de usuarios. En este punto, terminar la tarea y obtener un reembolso de créditos es la opción más segura. No incurrirás en ninguna pérdida. Si estás ansioso por continuar la tarea, sugerimos esperar un tiempo antes de solicitar a Manus que continúe.

Preguntas frecuentes relacionadas comunes:

*   ¿Por qué ocurre el error 10091?

*   ¿Puedo continuar mi tarea después del error 10091?
    
*   ¿Es seguro terminar una tarea?
    
*   ¿Cuándo ocurre generalmente el error 10091?
    
*   ¿Incurriré en alguna pérdida con el error 10091?
    
*   ¿Qué es la terminación por carga alta?

¿Qué puedo hacer si encuentro el error High Load Termination/10091 sin ninguna ventana emergente?

¿Qué puedo hacer si encuentro el error High Load Termination/10091 sin ninguna ventana emergente?
=================================================================================================

Aprenda a manejar el error High Load Termination/10091 sin una ventana emergente en Manus.

Actualizado hace más de 2 semanas

Este error ocurre generalmente cuando hay un alto volumen de acceso de usuarios. En este punto, terminar la tarea y obtener un reembolso de créditos es la opción más segura. No incurrirá en ninguna pérdida. Si está ansioso por continuar la tarea, le sugerimos esperar un tiempo antes de solicitar a Manus que continúe. Optimizaremos este problema lo antes posible para asegurar que los usuarios tengan una mejor experiencia.

Actualmente, proporcionamos esta ventana emergente para los usuarios cuyas Tareas son terminadas debido a una alta carga, permitiéndoles elegir si continuar o detenerse y recibir un reembolso de créditos.

# What happens to my credits after canceling or letting my Manus subscription expire? | Manus Help Center

[Skip to main content](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12268225-what-happens-to-my-credits-after-canceling-or-letting-my-manus-subscription-expire#main-content)

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12268225-what-happens-to-my-credits-after-canceling-or-letting-my-manus-subscription-expire#h_b30244554f)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12268225-what-happens-to-my-credits-after-canceling-or-letting-my-manus-subscription-expire#h_8e76a52932)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12268225-what-happens-to-my-credits-after-canceling-or-letting-my-manus-subscription-expire#h_f558c01150)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12268225-what-happens-to-my-credits-after-canceling-or-letting-my-manus-subscription-expire#h_f0cdae07b1)

[All Collections](https://help.manus.im/en/)

[Billing](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/13760762-billing)

[Credits & Usage](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/15919440-credits-usage)

What happens to my credits after canceling or letting my Manus subscription expire?

What happens to my credits after canceling or letting my Manus subscription expire?
===================================================================================

Learn what happens to your Manus credits when you cancel or let your subscription expire.

Updated over 3 weeks ago

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12268225-what-happens-to-my-credits-after-canceling-or-letting-my-manus-subscription-expire#h_b30244554f)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12268225-what-happens-to-my-credits-after-canceling-or-letting-my-manus-subscription-expire#h_8e76a52932)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12268225-what-happens-to-my-credits-after-canceling-or-letting-my-manus-subscription-expire#h_f558c01150)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12268225-what-happens-to-my-credits-after-canceling-or-letting-my-manus-subscription-expire#h_f0cdae07b1)

Understanding what happens to your credits after you cancel or let your Manus subscription expire is essential to make the most of your membership benefits. Here’s a detailed guide:

Impact of Subscription Cancellation on Credits
==============================================

When your Manus subscription is canceled or expires, the following occurs:

*   All membership benefits, including access to credits, are terminated as soon as the subscription ends.
    
*   Any unused credits remaining from monthly allocations are reset to 0 once the subscription cycle ends.
    
*   For users with a seven-day free trial, if you cancel your subscription before the charge, there will be no charge incurred. If you cancel your subscription after being charged, there will be no refund, and only the next renewal will be cancelled.
    

Use of Monthly and Event Credits
================================

*   **Monthly Credits**: These are tied directly to your active subscription. Once your subscription expires, any leftover monthly credits will no longer be available.
    
*   **Event Credits**: These credits can only be used with an active paid subscription. If your account switches to a Free membership or the subscription lapses, these credits become inactive.
    

Reactivating Credits After Subscription Renewal
===============================================

If you renew your subscription or subscribe to a new membership plan, previously unused credits can be reactivated. However, monthly credits that were reset to 0 cannot be reinstated.

Recommendations for Credit Usage
================================

To avoid losing any credits, it’s highly recommended to:

*   Utilize all purchased credits within your subscription cycle.
    
*   Plan credit usage in advance, especially if you anticipate canceling your subscription or switching to a Free membership.
    

By understanding and following these guidelines, you can make effective use of your credits and prevent their deactivation.

Common related FAQs:

*   What happens to my monthly credits when my subscription expires?
    
*   What happens to my event credits after cancellation?
    
*   Can I reactivate my credits if I renew my subscription?
    
*   Can monthly credits be reinstated after renewal?
    
*   How can I avoid losing my credits?
    
*   When are my membership benefits terminated after cancellation/termination?
    
*   What should I do if I plan to cancel my subscription?
    
*   Are unused monthly credits reset when the subscription ends?

# ¿Qué puedo hacer si VS Code no funciona? | Manus Help Center

[Ir al contenido principal](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11813724-que-puedo-hacer-si-vs-code-no-funciona#main-content)

[Todas las colecciones](https://help.manus.im/es/)

[Función](http://help.manus.im/es/collections/13762621-funcion)

[Solución de problemas & Limitaciones](http://help.manus.im/es/collections/15921659-solucion-de-problemas-limitaciones)

¿Qué puedo hacer si VS Code no funciona?

¿Qué puedo hacer si VS Code no funciona?
========================================

Aprende a solucionar problemas de VS Code en Manus.

Actualizado hace más de 2 semanas

Implementamos esta función basándonos en la especificación RFC estándar. Es muy probable que el problema que encontraste se deba a que la configuración de seguridad del navegador es demasiado alta, lo que puede causar un comportamiento anormal bajo niveles de seguridad superiores. Puedes intentar cambiar a un navegador diferente.

Por cierto, utilizamos un mecanismo de cookies de dominio cruzado para autorizar el servidor de VS Code, el cual funciona bajo niveles de seguridad de navegador estándar. Si tu navegador impone alguna restricción a las cookies de dominio cruzado, esto puede llevar a fallos de autorización.

Preguntas frecuentes relacionadas comunes:

*   ¿Por qué no funciona VS Code?
    
*   ¿Qué debo hacer si VS Code presenta problemas?
    
*   ¿Está VS Code basado en la especificación RFC?
    
*   ¿Qué causa el comportamiento anormal en VS Code?
    
*   ¿Debería cambiar de navegador si VS Code no funciona?
    
*   ¿Cómo autoriza Manus al servidor de VS Code?
    
*   ¿Pueden las restricciones del navegador afectar a VS Code?
    
*   ¿Qué causa los fallos de autorización en VS Code?
    
*   ¿Funciona VS Code bajo niveles de seguridad estándar?
    
*   ¿Pueden las restricciones de cookies de dominio cruzado causar problemas?
    
*   ¿En qué especificación se basa VS Code?
    

* * *

[¿Cómo puedo tomar el control del navegador o VS Code de Manus?](http://help.manus.im/es/articles/11711218-como-puedo-tomar-el-control-del-navegador-o-vs-code-de-manus)

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/13185575-is-there-a-way-to-check-how-many-credits-a-task-will-cost-before-i-begin#h_89e219ad85)

Is there a way to check how many credits a task will cost before I begin?

Is there a way to check how many credits a task will cost before I begin?
=========================================================================

Understand how Manus credits are consumed, optimize your usage, and learn to recognize AI behaviors.

Updated over a week ago

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/13185575-is-there-a-way-to-check-how-many-credits-a-task-will-cost-before-i-begin#h_89e219ad85)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/13185575-is-there-a-way-to-check-how-many-credits-a-task-will-cost-before-i-begin#h_210f333034)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/13185575-is-there-a-way-to-check-how-many-credits-a-task-will-cost-before-i-begin#h_84864bc592)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/13185575-is-there-a-way-to-check-how-many-credits-a-task-will-cost-before-i-begin#h_859218e98d)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/13185575-is-there-a-way-to-check-how-many-credits-a-task-will-cost-before-i-begin#h_895e16cd73)

Understanding Manus’ Credits Consumption and AI Behavior
--------------------------------------------------------

This article provides a comprehensive overview of how credits are utilized within the Manus platform and offers clarification on certain AI behaviors, such as hallucinations. A clear understanding of these aspects will enable users to leverage Manus more effectively and manage their interactions with greater efficiency.

The Mechanics of Credit Consumption
-----------------------------------

At present, Manus does not possess the capability to autonomously judge or regulate the consumption of credits. The quantity of credits utilized during each interaction is contingent upon the intricacy of the assigned task.

For a more detailed explanation of the credits system, we encourage you to consult our official help center article on credits, as well as our official Credits Usage document at the following link: [https://manus.im/help/credits](https://manus.im/help/credits)
.

**Strategies for Optimizing Credit Usage**
------------------------------------------

Should you observe that your credits are being expended at a rapid rate, the following recommendations may assist in optimizing your usage:

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Strategy | Description |
| Task Decomposition | Instead of issuing a series of instructions within a single, protracted conversation, it is advisable to deconstruct complex tasks into smaller, more focused sub-tasks. The greater the contextual load Manus is required to process, the higher the corresponding execution cost. |
| Initial Precision | Articulating your requirements with a high degree of precision at the outset of a conversation can significantly reduce the overall context length, thereby conserving credit consumption. |
| Detailed Instructions | Providing instructions that are both detailed and specific will facilitate a more efficient path to your desired outcome, minimizing the need for iterative clarification and the associated credit expenditure. |

**Future Enhancements in Credit Consumption Transparency**
----------------------------------------------------------

From a user experience standpoint, we recognize the universal desire for real-time visibility into credit consumption, as well as the aspiration for pre-task estimations of credit expenditure. Our product management team has identified this as a key area for improvement and is diligently working toward a solution. We anticipate the rollout of new features to address this in the near future. Your continued support is greatly appreciated, and we encourage you to stay informed about future updates to Manus.

A Primer on AI Hallucinations
-----------------------------

AI hallucinations are defined as instances in which an artificial intelligence generates information that is either incorrect or entirely fabricated. Awareness of these potential occurrences is essential for the accurate interpretation of Manus's responses. The following table outlines common scenarios in which AI hallucinations may manifest:

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Scenario | Description |
| Promises Regarding Credit Consumption | Manus may, on occasion, generate statements concerning the number of credits a particular task will consume. As previously stated, the system is not yet equipped to provide accurate predictions of credit usage. Any such statements should be regarded as hallucinations rather than factual commitments. |
| Admitting to Systemic Problems | There may be instances where Manus appears to acknowledge a problem or a bug within its own systems. While the AI is designed to be conversational and helpful, it occasionally lacks self-awareness and the capacity for self-diagnosis of technical issues. These "admissions" are typically part of a programmed response to user-expressed frustration and should not be interpreted as a confirmation of a genuine system-wide malfunction. |
| Pledges of Unattainable Actions | Manus might occasionally make commitments to perform tasks that lie beyond its current operational capabilities. For instance, it might assert an ability to execute actions in the physical world, or guarantee a specific outcome that is not technically feasible. It is imperative that users critically evaluate the assertions made by the AI and maintain a clear understanding of the platform's inherent limitations. |
| Fabricated Content | This includes completely made-up information that does not exist - Inventing non-existent academic papers, false citation sources, or fictional historical events. |
| Logical Hallucinations | Manus might occasionally produce logical errors or contradictions in the reasoning process. This includes providing mutually contradictory conclusions within the same response. |

We trust that this article has provided valuable insights into the operational nuances of Manus. Our team remains steadfast in its commitment to the continuous improvement of the platform, with the goal of delivering a more transparent and reliable user experience. We thank you for your continued support.

*   How can I reduce my point consumption?
    
*   What makes a task complex?

¿Cómo puedo solicitar un reembolso de créditos?

¿Cómo puedo solicitar un reembolso de créditos?
===============================================

Aprenda cómo solicitar un reembolso de créditos de Manus cuando encuentre problemas o no esté satisfecho con los resultados.

Actualizado hace más de una semana

Si encuentra algún problema durante el uso o no está satisfecho con los resultados generados por Manus, apoyamos a los usuarios informando los problemas y reembolsaremos los créditos después de la verificación.

Para comprender mejor su escenario de conversación para la identificación de problemas y la solución de problemas, comparta sus enlaces de conversación con nosotros.

Intente hacer públicos los enlaces👇

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1887332705/49fd304e4c82309397abff74d368/image.png?expires=1766962800&signature=369ba39ff1bb0e659e55eee4e535fa57b4bc6da5181c3fb8078a793fcea57d63&req=dSgvEcp9n4ZfXPMW1HO4zdLo59Z3MPhy6jEoKw2Lv1PTLq5OUVVsELZt79dT%0AeQBR1qNGKnrnxAe6b1M%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1887332705/49fd304e4c82309397abff74d368/image.png?expires=1766962800&signature=369ba39ff1bb0e659e55eee4e535fa57b4bc6da5181c3fb8078a793fcea57d63&req=dSgvEcp9n4ZfXPMW1HO4zdLo59Z3MPhy6jEoKw2Lv1PTLq5OUVVsELZt79dT%0AeQBR1qNGKnrnxAe6b1M%3D%0A)

Manus respeta absolutamente la privacidad del usuario y garantizamos que su enlace compartido solo se utilizará para la investigación de problemas.

# ¿Qué puedo hacer cuando alcanzo el límite de la base de conocimiento? | Manus Help Center

[Ir al contenido principal](https://help.manus.im/es/articles/11813718-que-puedo-hacer-cuando-alcanzo-el-limite-de-la-base-de-conocimiento#main-content)

[Todas las colecciones](https://help.manus.im/es/)

[Función](http://help.manus.im/es/collections/13762621-funcion)

[Solución de problemas & Limitaciones](http://help.manus.im/es/collections/15921659-solucion-de-problemas-limitaciones)

¿Qué puedo hacer cuando alcanzo el límite de la base de conocimiento?

¿Qué puedo hacer cuando alcanzo el límite de la base de conocimiento?
=====================================================================

Aprende qué hacer cuando alcanzas un límite de la base de conocimiento de Manus.

Actualizado hace más de 2 semanas

Actualmente, la base de conocimiento del usuario está limitada a 100 entradas para usuarios Pro y 50 entradas para usuarios Free. Si encuentras problemas relacionados con alcanzar el límite, puedes filtrar las entradas en tu base de conocimiento según tus necesidades más importantes y recientes, y eliminar algunas entradas innecesarias. En el futuro, continuaremos optimizando la funcionalidad de la base de conocimiento basándonos en las necesidades y comentarios de los usuarios.

Para asegurar la calidad de las respuestas de Manus, se recomienda que optimices apropiadamente el contenido de tu base de conocimiento y evites exceder el límite, ya que tener demasiadas entradas puede afectar la calidad de respuesta del sistema.

Preguntas frecuentes relacionadas comunes:

*   ¿Cuál es el límite de la base de conocimiento para los usuarios Pro?
    
*   ¿Cuál es el límite de la base de conocimiento para los usuarios Free?
    
*   ¿Cómo puedo gestionar mi base de conocimiento cuando alcanzo el límite?
    
*   ¿Puedo eliminar entradas de la base de conocimiento?
    
*   ¿Optimizará Manus la funcionalidad de la base de conocimiento?
    
*   ¿Superar el límite afecta la calidad de la respuesta?
    
*   ¿Cómo debo filtrar las entradas de mi base de conocimiento?
    
*   ¿Qué debo priorizar al filtrar entradas?
    
*   ¿Existe una diferencia en los límites entre los usuarios Pro y Free?
    
*   ¿Cambiará el límite de la base de conocimiento en el futuro?

# What can I do if I encounter an internal server error (10091)? | Manus Help Center

[Skip to main content](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711263-what-can-i-do-if-i-encounter-an-internal-server-error-10091#main-content)

[All Collections](https://help.manus.im/en/)

[Feature](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/13762621-feature)

[Troubleshooting & Limitations](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/15921659-troubleshooting-limitations)

What can I do if I encounter an internal server error (10091)?

What can I do if I encounter an internal server error (10091)?
==============================================================

Learn how to handle error 10091 in Manus.

Updated over 2 weeks ago

Currently, we provide this tip for users whose tasks are terminated due to high load, allowing them to choose whether to continue or stop and receive a refund of credits.

[![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1603178045/3c0c52fc7434c21f379df6a3af5f/asynccode?expires=1766962800&signature=4833c7a691e529d627b9b76bb2a4356d9f77a6309baf17b770a935e8cc9efbe9&req=dSYnFch5lYFbXPMW1HO4zXzEOi7vrzA196vd0DV%2Bx9q1f8SlNOk5unNSoR0H%0Apnl18HCzuTkiDdKQZPo%3D%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1603178045/3c0c52fc7434c21f379df6a3af5f/asynccode?expires=1766962800&signature=4833c7a691e529d627b9b76bb2a4356d9f77a6309baf17b770a935e8cc9efbe9&req=dSYnFch5lYFbXPMW1HO4zXzEOi7vrzA196vd0DV%2Bx9q1f8SlNOk5unNSoR0H%0Apnl18HCzuTkiDdKQZPo%3D%0A)

This error usually occurs when there is a high volume of user access. At this point, terminating the task and obtaining a refund of credits is the safest option. You won't incur any loss. If you are eager to continue the task, we suggest waiting for a while before requesting Manus to proceed.

What is the current membership pricing for Manus?

What is the current membership pricing for Manus?
=================================================

Learn about monthly and annual plans, pricing locations, and how much you can save with annual subscriptions.

Updated over a week ago

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711111-what-is-the-current-membership-pricing-for-manus#h_c9bdaff16f)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711111-what-is-the-current-membership-pricing-for-manus#h_38148d742d)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711111-what-is-the-current-membership-pricing-for-manus#h_21fb3f149c)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11711111-what-is-the-current-membership-pricing-for-manus#h_2cc25c261a)

You can find our pricing through the [manus.im/home](http://manus.im/home)
 -> [https://manus.im/pricing](https://manus.im/pricing)
.

After entering the Manus homepage, scroll down to the bottom of the page to view our product pricing.

Currently, Manus offers Free & Pro & Team plan options to meet the needs of different users. Whether you are an individual user or a team user, Manus can provide you with efficient solutions.

**_\*Please note that Free users only have access to Manus 1.6 Lite in Agent Mode, while Pro users have access to Manus 1.6, Manus 1.6 Max, and Manus 1.6 Lite. Both Free and Pro users have access to Chat Mode._**

Here are the detailed contents of each plan:

【Free Plan Price: $0/month】
===========================

1.  Access to Chat Mode and Manus 1.6 Lite in Agent Mode.
    
2.  Features: Daily Refresh Credits: 300 credits provided daily for quickly answering simple questions.
    
3.  Concurrent Tasks: Supports 1 concurrent task.
    
4.  Scheduled Tasks: Supports 2 scheduled tasks.
    
5.  Use Cases: Suitable for individual users with low functional requirements to experience Manus's basic features.
    

【Pro Plan Price: Starting from $20/month (Enjoy a 17% discount with annual billing)】
====================================================================================

Free users can upgrade to a membership for more credits. Members who need additional credits can switch to a higher plan.

1.  Access to Chat Mode and Manus 1.6 Max, Manus 1.6, and Manus 1.6 Lite in Agent Mode.
    
2.  Features: Monthly Credits: Starting from 4,000 credits per month, supporting higher frequency usage needs.
    
3.  Advanced Research: Supports advanced research on any topic.
    
4.  Professional Website Deployment: Provides professional-level website deployment services.
    
5.  Slide Generation: Generates slides with deep insights and a clear structure.
    
6.  Wide Research: Performs better in high-intensity tasks.
    
7.  Task Quantity: Supports 20 concurrent tasks and 20 scheduled tasks.
    
8.  Beta Feature Early Access: Experience the latest features in advance.
    
9.  Use Cases: Suitable for users who need to conduct in-depth research and generate professional reports, helping to improve work efficiency.
    

【Team Plan Price: Starting from $40 per seat/month (Enjoy a 17% discount with annual billing)】
==============================================================================================

1.  Access to Chat Mode and Manus 1.6 Max, Manus 1.6, and Manus 1.6 Lite in Agent mode.
    
2.  Target Users: Team users who need collaboration and advanced management features.
    
3.  Features: Includes all features of the Pro plan.
    
4.  SSO (Single Sign-On): Provides more convenient login methods.
    
5.  Data Training Opt-Out: Supports opting out of data training to protect privacy.
    
6.  Team Usage Analytics: Provides analytical data on team usage.
    
7.  Internal Access Control: Better management of team permissions.
    
8.  Shared Slide Templates: Provides shared slide templates for teams to improve collaboration efficiency.
    
9.  Use Cases: Suitable for enterprise or team users who need team collaboration, data privacy protection, and advanced management features.
    

Everything is subject to what is displayed on the actual pricing page.

### Plan (Monthly):

Troubleshooting:
================

Question: What will happen to existing members under the new pricing plans?

*   Existing member users will still auto-renew with unchanged prices and can upgrade or downgrade to new plans. The original Basic and Plus plans have both been renamed to Pro.

# How does our AI agent's credit refund policy work? | Manus Help Center

[Skip to main content](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12992237-how-does-our-ai-agent-s-credit-refund-policy-work#main-content)

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12992237-how-does-our-ai-agent-s-credit-refund-policy-work#h_e76cb80134)

[Refunds](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/15919586-refunds)

How does our AI agent's credit refund policy work?

How does our AI agent's credit refund policy work?
==================================================

Learn about Manus AI agent's credit refund policy. Understand when refunds are issued for bugs and platform malfunctions, and the AI-powered review process.

Updated over a week ago

Table of contents

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12992237-how-does-our-ai-agent-s-credit-refund-policy-work#h_e76cb80134)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12992237-how-does-our-ai-agent-s-credit-refund-policy-work#h_4b175a6048)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12992237-how-does-our-ai-agent-s-credit-refund-policy-work#h_f2d0292be5)

[](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/12992237-how-does-our-ai-agent-s-credit-refund-policy-work#h_b2e8af3d96)

Understanding Our Credit Refund Policy
--------------------------------------

At Manus, we use a credit system to enable our AI agents to perform a wide range of tasks on your behalf. We are committed to ensuring that this system is fair and transparent. This article explains how our credit refund policy works, including the process for requesting a refund and the circumstances under which refunds are issued.

Our primary goal is to provide a reliable and effective service. If our platform fails to deliver due to a technical issue on our end, we believe you are entitled to a refund for the credits used on that task. All refund requests are carefully reviewed by a specialized AI agent and our Customer Success team to ensure a fair and consistent evaluation.

When Credit Refunds Are Issued
------------------------------

We will issue a full credit refund for a task if our investigation confirms that the issue was caused by a verifiable bug or platform malfunction. Our commitment is to ensure you only pay for tasks that are processed correctly by our systems.

**What qualifies as a bug?**

A bug is a technical error or fault in the Manus platform that prevents the AI agent from completing a task as expected or causes it to behave in an unintended way.

Examples of situations where a refund will be issued:

*   **Platform Error:** The AI agent fails to execute a task due to an internal server error, a tool malfunction, or an unexpected system crash.
    
*   **Tool Misuse:** The AI agent uses a tool incorrectly in a way that directly violates its documented instructions, leading to task failure.
    
*   **Incomplete Execution:** The AI agent stops mid-task without a valid reason (e.g., not due to hitting a limit or receiving a user stop command) and fails to deliver any results.
    

We sincerely apologize for any unpleasant experiences you may have encountered while using Manus.

AI-generated content may not always meet 100% satisfaction as different users have varying standards. You can provide instructions to Manus based on your goals and needs to generate corresponding content, and then continuously adjust and refine the output.

If you describe your requirements as precisely as possible at the very beginning of a conversation, it can help reduce the overall context length and credit consumption. A small tip for minimizing credit consumption: issuing more detailed, clear, and less ambiguous instructions and descriptions to Manus might help you achieve your desired results more quickly.

When Credit Refunds Are Not Issued
----------------------------------

While we aim to be fair, we cannot issue refunds for situations that fall outside the scope of a platform malfunction. This includes issues related to user-provided instructions, subjective satisfaction with the outcome, or the inherent limitations of AI.

Refunds are generally not issued in the following circumstances:

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Scenario | Description |
| Change of Mind | You decide you no longer need the task completed after the AI agent has already started or finished the work. Credits are consumed as the agent works, and this work cannot be undone. |
| Unclear Instructions | Your instructions were ambiguous, contradictory, or incomplete, leading the AI agent to make a reasonable interpretation that did not align with your unstated expectations. |
| Subjective Dissatisfaction | The AI agent completed the task as requested, but you are not satisfied with the creative or subjective aspects of the outcome (e.g., writing style, design choice, or analytical approach). |
| External Factors | The task fails due to issues with third-party websites, APIs, or services that are beyond Manus's control (e.g., a website is down, an external API returns an error). |
| Hitting Task Limits | The task was stopped because it reached a predefined safety or resource/knowledge base limit, which is a standard operational procedure. |

We encourage users to provide clear, specific, and detailed instructions to ensure the best possible outcome for their tasks.

The AI-Powered Refund Review Process
------------------------------------

To ensure fairness and accuracy, all credit refund requests are handled by a specialized AI agent that is trained to analyze task execution logs. This process is designed to be objective and thorough.

**How It Works**

1.  Request Submission: You submit/imply a refund request for a specific task and share a task link with us. To share your conversation/task link with us, you may refer to the screenshots below:
    
    [![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1887342446/ec08aac5a5f41a57b42a9ea655b1/image.png?expires=1766962800&signature=8bc10d77d52c91d29e93e7f11cf1d3320fe601f96eae3752376c2c9f0bf0ffae&req=dSgvEcp6n4VbX%2FMW1HO4zQzz%2BRIR5fxcYnABqyi6fEcd9PiSPoGJ1t%2BqaKDI%0A5PAH%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1887342446/ec08aac5a5f41a57b42a9ea655b1/image.png?expires=1766962800&signature=8bc10d77d52c91d29e93e7f11cf1d3320fe601f96eae3752376c2c9f0bf0ffae&req=dSgvEcp6n4VbX%2FMW1HO4zQzz%2BRIR5fxcYnABqyi6fEcd9PiSPoGJ1t%2BqaKDI%0A5PAH%0A)
    
    [![](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1887342207/cb75102bb5e39a51f0c7a9d0095b/image.png?expires=1766962800&signature=a434796c6fad2526fea8178fef186330352734168f5f76db21cac019b80f97f2&req=dSgvEcp6n4NfXvMW1HO4zVIJ36Y52zvQDHB2yv9CAI100Qq7JcjgtkuMyCXS%0AFllM%0A)](https://downloads.intercomcdn.com/i/o/k7n2hgls/1887342207/cb75102bb5e39a51f0c7a9d0095b/image.png?expires=1766962800&signature=a434796c6fad2526fea8178fef186330352734168f5f76db21cac019b80f97f2&req=dSgvEcp6n4NfXvMW1HO4zVIJ36Y52zvQDHB2yv9CAI100Qq7JcjgtkuMyCXS%0AFllM%0A)
    
2.  AI Review Initiated: Our system assigns your request to a review AI. This AI is granted temporary, read-only access to the complete execution history of the specified task, including all steps, tool inputs/outputs, and system logs.
    
3.  Thorough Analysis: The AI agent meticulously reviews the entire task history to identify any anomalies, errors, or deviations from expected behavior. It cross-references the agent's actions with our internal tool documentation and platform health logs to determine if a bug occurred.
    
4.  Decision: Based on its analysis, the AI makes a determination. If a bug is confirmed, a credit refund is processed automatically to your account.
    

**Please Be Patient During the Review**

This comprehensive review process is highly detailed and can take some time to complete. The AI agent must analyze potentially thousands of data points to make an accurate and fair decision.

We kindly ask for your patience while our AI agent completes its review. Rushing the process could lead to an inaccurate conclusion. You will be notified as soon as the review is complete and a decision has been made.

If you have further questions about our credit system or policies, please feel free to browse other articles in our help centre or contact our support team.

# What can I do when I reach the knowledge base limit? | Manus Help Center

[Skip to main content](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11813718-what-can-i-do-when-i-reach-the-knowledge-base-limit#main-content)

[All Collections](https://help.manus.im/en/)

[Feature](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/13762621-feature)

[Troubleshooting & Limitations](http://help.manus.im/en/collections/15921659-troubleshooting-limitations)

What can I do when I reach the knowledge base limit?

What can I do when I reach the knowledge base limit?
====================================================

Learn what to do when reaching a Manus knowledge base limit.

Updated over 2 weeks ago

Currently, the user knowledge base is limited to 100 entries for Pro users and 50 entries for Free users. If you encounter issues related to reaching the limit, you can filter the entries in your knowledge base based on your most important and recent needs, and delete some unnecessary entries. In the future, we will continue to optimize the knowledge base functionality based on user needs and feedback.

To ensure the quality of Manus responses, it is recommended that you appropriately streamline the content of your knowledge base and avoid exceeding the limit, as having too many entries may affect the system's response quality.

# What can I do if I encounter High Load Termination/10091 error without any pop-up window? | Manus Help Center

[Skip to main content](https://help.manus.im/en/articles/11813677-what-can-i-do-if-i-encounter-high-load-termination-10091-error-without-any-pop-up-window#main-content)
